    window.utag_data = window.utag_data || {};
 
                                                         window.utag_data.ad_sec1 = "lifestyle";
                                                                 window.utag_data.ad_sec2 = "home";
                                                                 window.utag_data.ad_pagetype = "homepage";
                                     
                                                         window.utag_data.net_content_type = "homepage";
                                                                 window.utag_data.net_pn = "homepage";
                                                                 window.utag_data.net_sec1 = "home";
                                     
                 
         window.NLM = window.NLM || {};
         window.NLM.tealiumEnv = "prod";
         window.NLM.tealiumConfig = {"events":{"print":"event9"},"variables":{"story":{"type":"eVar25","value":"module name: print"}}};
 
         if ( typeof tealium_route_override != 'undefined' ) {
             tealium_current_route = tealium_route_override;
         }
 
         window.NLM.tealiumPlaceAd = (function(block_name, src_selector, device_queries) {
             var device = 'desktop';
             logger.info('Processing dynamic ad placing for "' + block_name + '"');
 
             if (window.NLM.mobileDetect.tablet()) {
                 device = 'desktop'; // Not a bug. Tablet should get desktop ads http://dashboard.news.com.au/browse/NLMFP-1078
             } else if (window.NLM.mobileDetect.mobile()) { // Else if here is necessary. window.NLM.mobileDetect.mobile() returns a truthy value for tablets
                 device = 'mobile';
             }
 
             if (device == 'mobile'){
                 window.utag_data.disable_oop_ads = true;
             }
             logger.info('Placing ad blocks as per device: ' + device);
             var dst_selector = device_queries[device];
 
             // If there is no configuration defined for the device, exit the function.
             if (null == dst_selector) {
                 logger.warn('Destination selector is not set, skipping.');
                 return false;
             }
 
             var $src_element = jQuery(src_selector);
             var $dst_element = jQuery(dst_selector);
 
 			if ($dst_element.length === 0) {
 				return;
 			}
 
 			if ($src_element.length === 0) {
 				return;
 			}
 
 			$src_element.children().first().css({
 				'text-align': 'center',
 				'padding-bottom': '20px'
 			});
 
 			if ($src_element.html() === '') {
 				$dst_element.replaceWith($src_element);
 			} else {
 				$dst_element.replaceWith($src_element.html());
 				$src_element.remove();
 			}
 
 			$dst_element.attr('data-ks-original-position', block_name);
         });
 
         window.NLM = window.NLM || {};
         window.NLM.mobileDetect = new MobileDetect(window.navigator.userAgent);
 
                             
         
         window.NLM.mobileDetect = window.NLM.mobileDetect || new MobileDetect(window.navigator.userAgent);
 
                     window.NLM.tealiumPlaceAd('index_page_mrec1', 'div.ad-mrec:eq(0)', {"desktop":null,"mobile":"div.ad-mobile-pos1-homepage-after-lead-story-3","tablet":null});
         
         // Map adblocks only on mobile phones.
         if (window.NLM.mobileDetect.mobile() && (null === window.NLM.mobileDetect.tablet())) {
             var mapping = {"mrec":"m-mrec","banner":"m-banner","leader":"m-banner","halfpage":"m-mrec","article-half-post-p-pos-1":"m-mrec"};
             jQuery('.ad-block').each(function (i, adblock) {
                 var $adblock = jQuery(adblock);
                 _.each(mapping, function (val, key) {
                     var adblockClass = 'ad-' + key;
                     var adblockMobileClass = 'ad-' + val;
 
                     if ($adblock.hasClass(adblockClass)) {
                         $adblock.removeClass(adblockClass);
                         $adblock.addClass(adblockMobileClass);
                     }
                 });
             });
         }
